<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="border: none; padding: 0;">
<div class="NavHead" style="font-size: 105%; background: transparent; text-align: left; text-align:center;background-color:#efefef;">Lap leaders</div>
<ul class="NavContent" style="list-style: none none; margin-left: 0; text-align: center; font-size: 105%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; line-height: inherit;"><li style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0"><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_fad035be582cae72cb60decfda1dc1df"></map><img usemap="#timeline_fad035be582cae72cb60decfda1dc1df" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/fad035be582cae72cb60decfda1dc1df.png" /></div></li></ul>
</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2014 Canadian Grand Prix</b> (officially the <b>Formula 1 Grand Prix du Canada 2014</b>) was a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> motor race held at the <a href="/wiki/Circuit_Gilles_Villeneuve" title="Circuit Gilles Villeneuve">Circuit Gilles Villeneuve</a> in <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">Quebec</a>, on 8 June. It was the seventh race of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2014 Formula One World Championship">2014 Formula One World Championship</a> and the 45th time the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="Canadian Grand Prix">event</a> formed part of the series. <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull Racing</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> won the 70-lap race from sixth position. <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> finished in second position for <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> and Ricciardo's teammate <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> took third.
</p><p>Rosberg took the <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> by setting the fastest lap in qualifying. He held off his teammate <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> to lead the field into the first corner. The race was neutralised with the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a> on the same lap due to a crash between <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a> teammates <a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a>. Rosberg maintained the lead until his first <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit stop</a> on the 18th lap. Rosberg retook it from his teammate Hamilton on lap 19. Kinetic <a href="/wiki/Motor%E2%80%93generator" title="Motor–generator">motor–generator unit</a> failures slowed both Rosberg and Hamilton just after halfway through the race. Rosberg made a <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit stop</a> at the end of lap 44. Hamilton led that lap and the next before his own pit stop. Williams driver <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> took the lead for the following two laps and relinquished it back to Rosberg on the 48th lap. Ricciardo overtook <a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> of <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> for second on lap 66, and Rosberg two laps later. Competitive racing ended with the safety car's deployment on the final lap due to a first turn accident between Massa and Pérez that saw both drivers briefly hospitalised. Ricciardo took the first victory of his career and the first for an Australian driver since <a href="/wiki/2012_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2012 Formula One World Championship">2012</a>.
</p><p>The result increased Rosberg's lead in the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">Drivers' Championship</a> to 22 <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a> over his teammate Hamilton who retired with overheating rear brakes. Ricciardo's victory advanced him to third, demoted <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> to fourth and elevated Vettel to fifth. In the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championship</a>, Mercedes maintained its lead over Red Bull in second. Ferrari, Force India and <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> all maintained third to fifth with twelve races left in the season.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve,_May_29,_2018_SkySat_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve%2C_May_29%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Circuit_Gilles-Villeneuve,_May_29,_2018_SkySat_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Circuit_Gilles_Villeneuve" title="Circuit Gilles Villeneuve">Circuit Gilles Villeneuve</a> <i>(pictured in 2018)</i>, where the race was held.</div></div></div>
<p>The 2014 Canadian Grand Prix was the 7th of 19 races of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2014 Formula One World Championship">2014 Formula One World Championship</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CF1Race_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF1Race-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> and the 45th running of the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="Canadian Grand Prix">event</a> as part of the series.<sup id="cite_ref-GazettePreview_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GazettePreview-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> It was held at the 14-turn 4.361&#160;km (2.710&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Circuit_Gilles_Villeneuve" title="Circuit Gilles Villeneuve">Circuit Gilles Villeneuve</a> in <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">Quebec</a> on 8 June.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_tyres" title="Formula One tyres">Tyre</a> supplier <a href="/wiki/Pirelli" title="Pirelli">Pirelli</a> brought the yellow-banded soft compound and the red-banded supersoft compound tyres to the race.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingStats_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingStats-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Drag_reduction_system" title="Drag reduction system">drag reduction system</a> (DRS) had two activation zones for the race: one was on the main <a href="/wiki/Straight_(racing)" title="Straight (racing)">straight</a> linking turns 11 and 12 and the second was on the straight between the 13th and first corners.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> After the <a href="/wiki/2013_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Canadian Grand Prix">2013 round</a>, gravel to the outside of turn 10 and turn 13 was replaced by an asphalt surface. A barrier at turn 13 was moved further back and its debris fence updated. New guardrail posts were built so that there was no space more than 2&#160;m (6.6&#160;ft).<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After winning the preceding <a href="/wiki/2014_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Monaco Grand Prix">Monaco Grand Prix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">Drivers' Championship</a> with 122 <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>, four ahead of his teammate <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> in second. <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a> was in third with 61 points, and <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> was seven points behind him in fourth. <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a> rounded out the top five with 47 points.<sup id="cite_ref-points_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">Constructors' Championship</a>, Mercedes led with 240 points, and Red Bull was second with 99 points. Ferrari with 78 points and Force India with 67 points contended for third position. <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a> completed the top five with 52 points.<sup id="cite_ref-points_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg/170px-AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg/255px-AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg/340px-AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2386" data-file-height="2413" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:AlexanderRossiGoodwood2013.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Alexander_Rossi" title="Alexander Rossi">Alexander Rossi</a> <i>(pictured in 2013)</i> drove for <a href="/wiki/Caterham_F1" title="Caterham F1">Caterham</a> for the first time in 2014 during the first practice session.</div></div></div>
<p>Rosberg took the Drivers' Championship lead with a win at Monaco; his relationship with Hamilton diminished after the latter felt Rosberg prevented him from taking pole position. Both drivers spoke to each other before the event and Hamilton declared their relationship restored.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg said his relationship with Hamilton had not been affected and commented on the situation, "We're fighting every single race weekend, it's me against him and there's nobody else. So that definitely makes it more difficult and there's more at stake. There is the opportunity of winning the championship this year – that is the ultimate goal in racing – so there's a lot at stake."<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton had won in Canada three times in <a href="/wiki/2007_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2007 Canadian Grand Prix">2007</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2010 Canadian Grand Prix">2010</a> and <a href="/wiki/2012_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2012 Canadian Grand Prix">2012</a> and said that the track's long straights would help Mercedes, "We have a very good power curve on our engine, Mercedes have done the best job with the engines. Renault (Red Bull’s power-plant supplier) and Ferrari would have to have done an exceptional job coming into this weekend, in terms of that area, to be able to keep up with us on the straights."<sup id="cite_ref-GazettePreview_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GazettePreview-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>There was one change of driver for the first practice session. <a href="/wiki/2014_GP2_Series" title="2014 GP2 Series">GP2 Series</a> participant and <a href="/wiki/Caterham_F1" title="Caterham F1">Caterham</a> reserve driver <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Rossi" title="Alexander Rossi">Alexander Rossi</a> drove the <a href="/wiki/Caterham_CT05" title="Caterham CT05">CT05</a> in lieu of <a href="/wiki/Kamui_Kobayashi" title="Kamui Kobayashi">Kamui Kobayashi</a> for the first time in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In technical developments, Mercedes installed fins and turning vanes to the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes_F1_W05_Hybrid" title="Mercedes F1 W05 Hybrid">F1 W05 Hybrid</a>'s lower front wishbone on its front <a href="/wiki/Suspension_(vehicle)" class="mw-redirect" title="Suspension (vehicle)">suspension</a> and the rear section of its frontal <a href="/wiki/Disc_brake" title="Disc brake">brake ducts</a>. This was to improve airflow and lessen <a href="/wiki/Drag_(physics)" title="Drag (physics)">drag</a> to the inside of the front wheel.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Toro_Rosso" title="Scuderia Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> built new <a href="/wiki/Exhaust_system" title="Exhaust system">exhaust systems</a> for their two cars following the development of fractures from possible overheating that led to their retirements in Monaco.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On the <a href="/wiki/Williams_FW36" title="Williams FW36">FW36</a>, <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> mounted a duct over the top of its brake discs to divert airflow from the main duct to the outside of the caliper.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Ferrari tested a tighter-mounted engine cover that went to the inside of the rear tyres. It featured longer <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#S" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">sidepods</a> to better cool the <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_F14_T" title="Ferrari F14 T">F14 T</a> and removed <a href="/wiki/Downforce" title="Downforce">downforce</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> During practice, McLaren used a rear suspension blocker to replace some <a href="/wiki/Downforce" title="Downforce">downforce</a> lost on the <a href="/wiki/McLaren_MP4-29" title="McLaren MP4-29">MP4-29</a> with the lower rear wing's removal at the cost of including drag.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice">Practice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Practice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_(13125202644).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_%2813125202644%29.jpg/170px-Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_%2813125202644%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="247" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_%2813125202644%29.jpg/255px-Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_%2813125202644%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c1/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_%2813125202644%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="266" data-file-height="386" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez_(13125202644).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> missed qualifying after crashing in the third practice session.</div></div></div>
<p>Per the regulations for the 2014 season, three practice sessions were held, two 90-minute sessions on Friday and another 60-minute session on Saturday.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-regulations_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The first practice session was held under heavy cloud cover that threatened a heavy rain shower. <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> of Ferrari was fastest with a benchmark lap of 1 minute and 17.238 seconds. He was ahead of the Mercedes duo of Hamilton and Rosberg. The Red Bull duo of <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> and Ricciardo were fourth and sixth; they were separated by <a href="/wiki/Valtteri_Bottas" title="Valtteri Bottas">Valtteri Bottas</a> for Williams. <a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a>, his McLaren teammate <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Magnussen" title="Kevin Magnussen">Kevin Magnussen</a>, Ferrari driver <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> and Toro Rosso's <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a> rounded out the top ten fastest drivers.<sup id="cite_ref-FP1_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FP1-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> During the session, several drivers went off the circuit because of a low amount of <a href="/wiki/Grip_(auto_racing)" title="Grip (auto racing)">grip</a> and unable to get the optimum <a href="/wiki/Operating_temperature" title="Operating temperature">tyre temperature</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SkyFP1_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyFP1-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a> damaged a right <a href="/wiki/Tie_rod" title="Tie rod">track rod</a> on his <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a> from contact against a wall at turn four. Hülkenberg spun by putting his wheels in the grass at the turn eight <a href="/wiki/Chicane" title="Chicane">chicane</a>. Williams driver <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> stopped early with an <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_energy_recovery_system" title="Kinetic energy recovery system">ERS</a> battery issue.<sup id="cite_ref-FP1_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FP1-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SkyFP1_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyFP1-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the session, Ricciardo was summoned by the stewards and was reprimanded for the first time in the season; he was judged to have passed <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Pastor_Maldonado" title="Pastor Maldonado">Pastor Maldonado</a> in a potentially unsafe manner to other drivers in the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a> at the conclusion of practice.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton recorded the day's fastest lap, a one-minute and 16.118 seconds in the second practice session. His teammate Rosberg was second and Vettel third. The two Ferrari cars of Räikkönen and Alonso were fourth and fifth, Massa was sixth with his teammate Bottas seventh. Mangussen, Button and Vergne followed in the top ten. Several drivers again ran off the circuit during the session. A suspected fuel leak caused <a href="/wiki/Daniil_Kvyat" title="Daniil Kvyat">Daniil Kvyat</a> to end his running early after completing nine laps. Bianchi was restricted to three slow laps because of engine issues that would require an overnight change of engine.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The third practice session took place in warm weather conditions. Hamilton used the soft compound tyres to record the fastest time of 1 minute and 15.610 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP3_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP3-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Massa was second and Rosberg third. Alonso was fourth and his teammate Räikkönen sixth; Ricciardo separated the two in fifth. Bottas, Kvyat, Vergne and Vettel were in positions seven to ten.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> The session was <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Red_flag" title="Racing flags">red flagged</a> 15 minutes in when <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> had a loss of control at the rear of his <a href="/wiki/Sauber" class="mw-redirect" title="Sauber">Sauber</a>'s braking through the turn three and four chicane. He struck an outside barrier at its exit, causing damage to his car's left-rear.<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP3_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP3-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Sauber discovered its front was too heavily damaged; Gutiérrez would miss qualifying because the team's spare chassis had to be constructed for the race on Sunday.<sup id="cite_ref-GutierrezQuali_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GutierrezQuali-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Gutierrez_starts_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gutierrez_starts-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying">Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="206" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1890" data-file-height="2285" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_Stars_and_Cars_2014_2_amk_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> secured the seventh <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> of his career.</div></div></div>
<p>Saturday afternoon's <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Q" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">qualifying session</a> was divided into three parts.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-regulations_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The first part ran for 18 minutes, eliminating cars that finished the session 17th or below. The <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107% rule</a> was in effect, requiring drivers to reach a time within 107 per cent of the quickest lap to qualify. The second session lasted 15 minutes, eliminating cars that finished 11th to 16th. The final session ran for 12 minutes and determined <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> to tenth. Cars who progressed to the final session were not allowed to change tyres for the race's start, using the tyres with which they set their quickest lap times in the second session.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The weather was sunny with the asphalt temperature 47&#160;°C (117&#160;°F).<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg led the third session to take his second consecutive pole position, his third of the season, and the seventh of his career with a 1-minute and 14.874 seconds lap.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> He was joined on the <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a>'s front row by his teammate Hamilton who was 0.079 seconds slower after driver errors at turns six and eight and slower traffic delayed him.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Vettel took more risks in his driving and placed third in the final seconds of qualifying.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-VettelQuali_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VettelQuali-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Traffic affected Bottas' front tyre warming and left him in fourth.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> His teammate Massa in fifth had a front-left brake temperature issue that locked his front wheel at turn one.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Ricciardo in sixth was beaten in qualifying by his teammate Vettel for the second time in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-VettelQuali_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VettelQuali-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> The Ferrari cars of Alonso and Räikkönen lacked grip and took seventh and tenth; they were separated by Vergne and Button after the latter altered his car's balance.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hülkenberg in 11th was the fastest driver not to qualify in the top ten. He was joined by Magnussen in 12th and Hülkenberg's teammate <a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> was 13th.<sup id="cite_ref-QResults_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QResults-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> 14th-placed <a href="/wiki/Romain_Grosjean" title="Romain Grosjean">Romain Grosjean</a> could not better his lap because he missed an opportunity to set another lap one second after the second session ended. Brake and handling difficulties left Kvyat in 15th position.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Sauber's <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a> used two sets of super soft compound tyres in the first session and set one timed lap in the second session to qualify 16th.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Maldonado failed to advance beyond the first session due to a turbocharger intake problem.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Penalties_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Penalties-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He stopped at the exit of turn three after his engineers asked him to stop.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MALReprimand_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MALReprimand-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> 18th-placed <a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a> relied on a lap he established on his first attempt because qualifying was stopped for an accident in the first session.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> His teammate Bianchi in 19th could not emerge on track for a second try because his car failed to start.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Kobayashi had an improved balance on his Caterham and went faster on his final attempt to take 20th;<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_34-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Ericsson" title="Marcus Ericsson">Marcus Ericsson</a> in the second Caterham took 21st and caused a stoppage in the first session with a crash at the exit of the first chicane with 16 seconds to go.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportQuali_33-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportQuali-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-qualifying">Post-qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Post-qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The stewards gave Maldonado his first reprimand of the season because he did not refit his <a href="/wiki/Steering_wheel" title="Steering wheel">steering wheel</a> after vacating his car as required by the Formula One regulations at the exit of turn three.<sup id="cite_ref-MALReprimand_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MALReprimand-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Gutiérrez was allowed to start the race at the stewards discretion for meeting time requirements in practice.<sup id="cite_ref-Gutierrez_starts_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gutierrez_starts-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He was required to begin from the pit lane because Sauber changed the <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> and the chassis of his car as a result of his third practice accident. Kobayashi incurred a five-place grid penalty for changing his car's gearbox.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Penalties_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Penalties-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying_classification">Qualifying classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Qualifying classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The fastest lap in each of the three sessions is denoted in <b>bold</b> and the winner of <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> is indicated by a <img alt="double-dagger" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f9/Double-dagger-14-plain.png" decoding="async" width="9" height="14" data-file-width="9" data-file-height="14" />.
</p>

<dl><dt>Notes</dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> &#160;— <a href="/wiki/Kamui_Kobayashi" title="Kamui Kobayashi">Kamui Kobayashi</a> was imposed a five-place grid penalty for a <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> change.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Penalties_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Penalties-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_2"><b><a href="#ref_2">^2</a></b></span> &#160;— <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> did not take part in qualifying because his team was unable to repair his damaged car during the Saturday morning practice session in time.<sup id="cite_ref-GutierrezQuali_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GutierrezQuali-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He was allowed to start the race on the stewards' discretion.<sup id="cite_ref-Gutierrez_starts_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gutierrez_starts-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_3"><b><a href="#ref_3">^3</a></b></span> &#160;— Gutiérrez began from the pit lane because his car's gearbox and chassis were changed as a result of his accident during the final practice session.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Penalties_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Penalties-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Weather forecasts expected the race to be partially cloudy and warm;<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> conditions in itself were sunny. The air temperature was between 27 to 28&#160;°C (81 to 82&#160;°F) and the track temperature ranged from 44 to 49&#160;°C (111 to 120&#160;°F);<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingStats_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingStats-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Every driver from first to tenth began on the supersoft compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> When the race commenced at 14:00 local time,<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton made a faster start than his teammate Rosberg. The latter locked up entering the first corner and drifted wide in front of Hamilton as he fended off the former to the right.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> That put Hamilton onto some grass and allowed Vettel into second.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> At the entry to turn three, Chilton lost control of the rear of his Marussia,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">oversteered</a> into the car of his teammate Bianchi.<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi was launched airborne as his and Chilton's wheels interlocked. He spun into a barrier beside the track.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Bianchi was unhurt and he and Chilton retired. The accident prompted the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>'s deployment since <a href="/wiki/Motorsport_marshal" title="Motorsport marshal">track marshals</a> were needed to clear oil and debris laid on the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Max_Chilton_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Max_Chilton_2.jpg/170px-Max_Chilton_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="236" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Max_Chilton_2.jpg/255px-Max_Chilton_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Max_Chilton_2.jpg/340px-Max_Chilton_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2113" data-file-height="2931" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Max_Chilton_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a> <i>(pictured in 2013)</i> retired in a first-lap accident with his teammate <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>The field conserved fuel under the safety car,<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> which was withdrawn at the end of lap seven.<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On lap eight, Rosberg immediately drew clear from Vettel whose Red Bull car was slower by about 10&#160;km/h (6.2&#160;mph) on a straight.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Pérez passed Button on the approach to the final chicane for tenth on that lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On the next lap, a turbocharger connector pipe failure on Ericsson's car prompted his retirement in the pit lane to prevent engine damage.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNQuotes_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNQuotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Kvyat oversteered and spun at turn one on the tenth lap; he fell to the rear of the field.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On the same lap, Hamilton used DRS to pass Vettel into the last chicane for second position.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Sixth-placed Ricciardo was delayed by the Williams pair of Bottas and Massa, whom he could not pass due to a slower pace on a straight. Behind him, Vergne delayed the Ferrari pair of Alonso and Räikkönen, Pérez and Button. Pérez's super soft compound tyres began degrading by around laps 13 and 14. Ricciardo made a pit stop at the conclusion of lap 13 in his attempt to pass both of the Williams drivers.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Williams responded by calling Bottas into the pit lane for the soft compound tyres on lap 15. The same was done with his teammate Massa on the next lap.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Vettel was about six seconds behind Hamilton by his own pit stop on the lap for the soft compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On the 17th lap,<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Alonso made a pit stop and his higher speed moved him past Vergne for seventh.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg was more than two seconds ahead of Hamilton,<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> when he entered the pit lane one lap later.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton took the lead on lap 18 and maintained it before his own pit stop on lap 19.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg clipped a kerb on the inside of turn four and lost control at the rear on that lap; he narrowly avoided contact with a barrier and continued.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, Rosberg led with Hamilton second and the Force India duo of Pérez and Hülkenberg third and fourth. Vettel's slower pace allowed Bottas and Ricciardo to draw closer.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On the 21st lap, Kvyat illegally drove across the final run-off area to avoid an overtake by Räikkönen.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Maldonado retired with a loss of engine power on the following lap.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNQuotes_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNQuotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg/170px-Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="204" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg/255px-Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg/340px-Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2827" data-file-height="3399" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2014_China.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> <i>(pictured in 2014)</i> retired with overheating brakes after 47 laps.</div></div></div>
<p>During the 23rd lap, a loss of rear car control put Vettel wide during an attempted pass on Hülkenberg at the hairpin.<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> After a half spin at turn one lap 25, a rear-left wheel problem caused Kobayashi to retire after the first chicane.<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> As Hamilton <a href="/wiki/Drafting_(aerodynamics)" title="Drafting (aerodynamics)">slipstreamed</a> Rosberg on the main straight that lap,<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> his teammate locked his tyres into the final chicane and cut the corner.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> The stewards investigated Rosberg;<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> he was not penalised.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton's race engineer Pete Bonnington advised the former not to take risks.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingStats_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingStats-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Further down the field, Massa passed Alonso on the outside through the first and second turns for eighth on the 27th lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton drew to within less than a second behind Rosberg on lap 28 and had DRS available the following lap.<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> In the meantime, Button overtook Kvyat around the inside at the hairpin for 12th and Vettel held off Bottas at the final chicane.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Pérez in third managed his super soft tyres enough to prompt Force India to extend his stint on them.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On lap 35, he made a pit stop to switch to the soft compound tyres and rejoined the circuit in 10th.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bottas entered the pit lane from fifth on lap 36 in his attempt to pass Vettel. Red Bull responded by bringing Vettel in on the next lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton had drawn close to his teammate Rosberg; Mercedes observed warm temperatures on both cars' engine control systems on the kinetic <a href="/wiki/Motor%E2%80%93generator" title="Motor–generator">motor–generator units</a>. Hamilton's failed into turn ten on lap 36 and Rosberg's shut down on the approach to turn one on lap 37, losing their engines 160&#160;hp (120&#160;kW).<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingStats_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingStats-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> That lowered their top speed on the straight by 32&#160;km/h (20&#160;mph) and were four seconds a lap slower than before after instructions to restart the electric control systems were unsuccessful.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Hülkenberg made his pit stop on lap 41 and Williams put the third-placed Massa on a one-stop strategy due to Mercedes' reduced pace.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg entered the pit lane on lap 44;<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> a delay with the installation of his left-front tyre elevated Hamilton to the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg/170px-Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="296" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg/255px-Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg/340px-Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="444" data-file-height="772" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Daniel_Ricciardo_2015_Malaysia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> <i>(pictured in 2015)</i> took his maiden career victory and the first for an Australian since <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> in 2012.</div></div></div>
<p>Hamilton's second pit stop on lap 46 overheated his rear brake discs,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> as Massa took the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> An error from Hamilton at the hairpin that lap allowed Rosberg to claim second from his teammate.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton then slipstreamed back past with DRS; he ran onto a run-off area at the final corner,<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and passed Rosberg, before relinquishing second position to his teammate.<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> He ran off the track twice more,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> and was retired in the pit lane at the start of lap 48.<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Tyre wear on Massa's car prompted Williams to revert to a two-stop strategy.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> He entered the pit lane at the end of that lap.<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg retook the lead on the following lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes told him to go faster in the first sector to prevent Pérez from using DRS on the straight.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On lap 49, Kvyat retired with a <a href="/wiki/Drive_shaft" title="Drive shaft">drivetrain</a> fault at the hairpin.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNQuotes_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNQuotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On the 57th lap, Bottas' had tyres that were 12 laps older than his teammate Massa's.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Bottas locked his <a href="/wiki/Flat_spot" title="Flat spot">flat-spotted</a> tyres at the hairpin to allow his teammate Massa past. He then used DRS to overtake Hülkenberg;<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Massa passed Bottas on that lap.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Massa passed Hülkenberg for fifth before the final chicane on that lap.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He drew closer to Vettel and Ricciardo on lap 57,<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and set the race's <a href="/wiki/Fastest_lap" title="Fastest lap">fastest lap</a> on the following lap, at 1 minute and 18.504 seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingStats_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingStats-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> On lap 60, Alonso on the inside overtook Bottas for seventh between turns one and two.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Bottas lost eighth to Button soon after.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Grosjean retired with a broken rear wing on the following lap.<sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNQuotes_50-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNQuotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On lap 64, Vettel narrowly avoided hitting the rear of his teammate Ricciardo under braking for the hairpin. Vettel ran wide to prevent a collision, which allowed Massa to turn onto the inside line as Vettel jerked in turn 11. Massa gained on Vettel on the long straight; he did not pass him because he forgot to use DRS.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In the meantime, Pérez had rear brake problems.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On the 66th lap, Ricciardo used DRS, and steered to the outside to pass Pérez for second entering turn one.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> He went onto the grass at the corner.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_52-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> That caused Vettel to nearly hit Pérez's car in the following <a href="/wiki/Accordion_effect" title="Accordion effect">concertina effect</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ricciardo lowered Rosberg's lead to seven-tenths of a second between laps 66 and 67.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Gutiérrez entered the pit lane with an energy storage system failure on the 67th lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNQuotes_50-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNQuotes-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On the back straight at lap 68, Ricciardo used DRS to pass Rosberg for the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> On the next lap, Pérez went off the <a href="/wiki/Racing_line" title="Racing line">racing line</a> and Vettel found space to overtake him for third at the end of the back straight.<sup id="cite_ref-GuardianLive_47-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GuardianLive-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DTLive_48-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTLive-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Pérez was slow on the start/finish straight from having an untidy exit out of the final corner.<sup id="cite_ref-MagazineReport_49-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MagazineReport-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On the final lap,<sup id="cite_ref-GPUpdateRace_51-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPUpdateRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Massa's front right tyre and Pérez's left-rear wheel collided.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLive_45-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLive-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Pérez rammed into a barrier at 32<a href="/wiki/G-force" title="G-force">G</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-AMUSPERMASCrash_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AMUSPERMASCrash-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> as Massa narrowly avoided collecting Vettel en route into a tyre wall in a 27G impact.<sup id="cite_ref-MASPERCrash_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MASPERCrash-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The safety car was deployed to neutralise the race and Ricciardo took his first career victory, the first for an Australian since <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> won the <a href="/wiki/2012_British_Grand_Prix" title="2012 British Grand Prix">2012 British Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg finished second and Vettel third. Off the podium, Button, Hülkenberg, Alonso, Bottas, Vergne, Magnussen, Räikkönen, Pérez, Massa, Sutil and Gutiérrez were the final finishers.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCLive_46-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCLive-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-race">Post-race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Post-race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>At the podium interviews,<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> conducted by the <a href="/wiki/1995_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Canadian Grand Prix">1995 winner</a> of the race <a href="/wiki/Jean_Alesi" title="Jean Alesi">Jean Alesi</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Ricciardo said he was in shock over his first career win, "This is ridiculous! Lots of Aussie flags, that’s nice... It’s just an amazing feeling right now, I’m really grateful for this. Thanks everyone."<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg stated he had no knowledge of his surroundings after his second pit stop as he was too focused on his horsepower disadvantage. His compatriot Vettel congratulated his teammate Ricciardo on winning and said it was "a very positive day".<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> In the subsequent press conference, Ricciardo said he believed that more confidence and familiarity with the Formula One community helped him to win the Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg said he had to cool his brakes after his kinetic motor–generator unit failed, "I lost a lot of power on the straights. At the same time, taking those things into consideration, I was just pushing flat out, qualifying laps, one after another and managing to stay ahead of that pack behind me until two laps from the end."<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Vettel said he felt Red Bull had been fortunate after several issues early in the season and finishing the race ahead one of the Mercedes, "I think that’s a very, very positive day for us."<sup id="cite_ref-Interviews_56-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Interviews-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg/170px-Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg/255px-Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg/340px-Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Perez_2016_Malaysia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> <i>(pictured in 2016)</i> was given a five-place grid penalty for the <a href="/wiki/2014_Austrian_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Austrian Grand Prix">Austrian Grand Prix</a> because he was deemed to have caused an accident with <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> on the final lap.</div></div></div>
<p>Pérez and Massa were unhurt and were transported to the circuit's medical centre. They were later airlifted to the <a href="/wiki/H%C3%B4pital_du_Sacr%C3%A9-C%C5%93ur_de_Montr%C3%A9al" title="Hôpital du Sacré-Cœur de Montréal">Sacre Coeur hospital</a> for a pre-cautionary check-up because their crashes registered enough of a G-force to activate their car's medical alarm.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PERPenalty_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PERPenalty-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> The collision was referred to the stewards and Pérez incurred a five place grid penalty for the season's next race in <a href="/wiki/2014_Austrian_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Austrian Grand Prix">Austria</a> because they deemed him to have made an illegal manoeuvre that caused the crash.<sup id="cite_ref-PERPenalty_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PERPenalty-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> At the medical centre, Massa told Pérez of his disappointment with his driving and added he "needs to learn".<sup id="cite_ref-MASPERCrash_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MASPERCrash-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He criticised the stewards' penalty because of the severity of the accident that nearly saw him collect Vettel. Pérez said he maintained his braking sequence and line prior to the crash,
</p>
<blockquote><p>"There was plenty of space on the left of my car to attempt a clean overtake, and I cannot understand why he had to scrape by. I watched several replays of the incident and I can’t help but notice how Felipe turns right just before he hits me. I can only think he must have changed his mind and wanted to rejoin the racing line. His misjudgment cost us a big amount of points".<sup id="cite_ref-MASPERCrash_55-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MASPERCrash-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup></p></blockquote>
<p>The Force India team and its manager Andy Stevenson felt there was a conspiracy against them as one of the stewards was Pérez's former manager and <a href="/wiki/IndyCar_Series" title="IndyCar Series">IndyCar Series</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Adri%C3%A1n_Fern%C3%A1ndez" title="Adrián Fernández">Adrián Fernández</a>, who ended his partnership with Pérez in 2012. <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">FIA</a> Race Director <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a> dismissed the idea of a conspiracy as "nonsense". He commented Fernández would serve as the driver representative at the <a href="/wiki/2014_Russian_Grand_Prix" title="2014 Russian Grand Prix">Russian Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AMUSPERMASCrash_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AMUSPERMASCrash-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 20 June, the stewards called a meeting to review driver testimony and <a href="/wiki/Telemetry" title="Telemetry">telemetry</a> from Pérez. The FIA elected to uphold the stewards' decision on the basis that there was no purpose on which to change it.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The stewards also reviewed the accident between Marussia teammates Chilton and Bianchi on the first lap. Chilton incurred a three-place grid penalty for the upcoming Austrian Grand Prix for being deemed at fault for the accident.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Chilton said he believed Bianchi caused the crash by braking later than him on the outside. He believed additional television footage would have shown his teammate was responsible. Bianchi stated his belief he did not brake too late and had provided Chilton with space to drive past.<sup id="cite_ref-CHIBIACrash_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CHIBIACrash-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Both drivers spoke to each other on the morning of 19 June and they agreed to move on from the crash.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rosberg, who drove onto the run-off area on lap 25, stated his belief that the regulations on minor driver errors needed to be clarified to stop automatic steward investigations on such incidents, "It is worth discussing, because it going to the stewards is a bit strange. It is something that we all agreed among ourselves, and especially that the first time you can maybe get a warning, but you cannot do it three times in a row."<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports_F1" title="Sky Sports F1">Sky Sports F1</a></i> pundits <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Herbert" title="Johnny Herbert">Johnny Herbert</a> and <a href="/wiki/Martin_Brundle" title="Martin Brundle">Martin Brundle</a> believed Rosberg was fortunate not to receive a penalty. Their colleague <a href="/wiki/Damon_Hill" title="Damon Hill">Damon Hill</a> said a warning was justified.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> After his retirement from the race, Hamilton admitted he required a form similar to his four wins in a row earlier in the season to retake the lead in the Drivers' Championship, "It is going to take a lot, four wins. I just can’t believe that my car stops and the other doesn’t. Two DNFs is not easy but I have caught up before and I will catch up again."<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rosberg left Canada with an increased lead of 22 points over his teammate Hamilton in the Drivers' Championship. Ricciardo's victory elevated him to third. Alonso's seventh-place finish dropped him to fourth. Vettel rounded out the top five.<sup id="cite_ref-points_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In the Constructors' Championship, Mercedes maintained its lead with 258 points. Red Bull remained in second with 139 points. Ferrari's hold on third place was reduced by one point over Force India in fourth. McLaren drew closer to Force India by four points with twelve races remaining in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-points_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-points-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Race_classification">Race classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014_Canadian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Race classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
